SELECT o."Id", o."CreatedDate", o."GuestEmail", o."GuestName", o."TotalPrice", s."Id", s."OrderId", s."Price", s."ProductId", s."ProductId1", s."Quantity", s."Id0", s."CategoryId", s."LowStockThreshold", s."Name", s."Price0", s."QuantityInStock"
FROM "Orders" AS o
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT o0."Id", o0."OrderId", o0."Price", o0."ProductId", o0."ProductId1", o0."Quantity", p."Id" AS "Id0", p."CategoryId", p."LowStockThreshold", p."Name", p."Price" AS "Price0", p."QuantityInStock"
    FROM "OrderItems" AS o0
    INNER JOIN "Products" AS p ON o0."ProductId" = p."Id"
) AS s ON o."Id" = s."OrderId"
ORDER BY o."Id", s."Id"

FROM "Orders" AS o
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT o0."Id", o0."OrderId", o0."Price", o0."ProductId", o0."ProductId1", o0."Quantity", p."Id" AS "Id0", p."CategoryId", p."LowStockThreshold", p."Name", p."Price" AS "Price0", p."QuantityInStock"
    FROM "OrderItems" AS o0
    INNER JOIN "Products" AS p ON o0."ProductId" = p."Id"
) AS s ON o."Id" = s."OrderId"
ORDER BY o."Id", s."Id"
